GT is the fixed function  
\[
0.156062620221068\,\sin(t)\;-\;0.372947617362308\,v\,e^{-|x|}.
\]
So any matching candidate must be exactly “(pure sinusoid in \(t\) only) + (term linear in \(v\) times \(e^{k|x|}\) with \(k=-1\))”, with **no extra dependence** on \(x\) (outside \(|x|\) in the exponential), no extra dependence on \(v\) (nonlinear or denominators), and no extra \(t\)-dependence multiplying the \(v\)-term.

Also note trig phase: \(A\cos(\omega t+\phi)\) can equal \(A\sin(t)\) by choosing \(\omega=1\) and \(\phi=-\pi/2\) (or equivalent).

### 1
Has extra terms \(c3 v x^{c4}\), \(c7 v\), etc. You could set those coefficients to 0, leaving \(c0\cos(\cdot)+c5 v e^{c6|x|}\). That can match by phase-shifting cosine to sine and setting \(c6=-1\), \(c5=-0.3729...\), \(c0=0.1560...\). **Match possible.**
